ReFrame logs

1. ReFrame scheduler script

#!/bin/bash
#SBATCH --job-name="rfm_RegressionTest_e1c6da50"
#SBATCH --ntasks=2560
#SBATCH --ntasks-per-node=128
#SBATCH --cpus-per-task=1
#SBATCH --output=rfm_job.out
#SBATCH --error=rfm_job.err
#SBATCH --exclusive
#SBATCH --partition=cpu
#SBATCH --threads-per-core=1
#SBATCH --time=0-00:30:0
module load OpenMPI/4.1.5-GCC-12.3.0
srun --cpus-per-task=1 singularity exec -B"/ceph/hpc/home/euvincentc/actions-runner/_work/bench.ktirio.fr/bench.ktirio.fr/build/reframe/stage/vega/cpu/default/RegressionTest_e1c6da50:/rfm_workdir" --home /exa5/data/d2024d05-047-users/euvincentc/apptainer_home --bind /exa5/data/d2024d05-047-users/euvincentc/inputdataset:/input_data --env OMP_NUM_THREADS=1 --bind /opt:/opt /ceph/hpc/home/euvincentc/images_sif/kub_feature-cem_partitioning-sif feelpp_kub_cem --config-files /input_data/kub/idealHeaters.cfg --cem.simulator.sun.filename=/input_data/kub/simulators/Sun.fmu --cem.simulator.lod0.modelisation.maxfloors=10 --cem.preprocessing.dataregistry.directory=/input_data/kub_benchmark/3km/preprocessing --cem.weather.filename=/input_data/kub/Paris/weather.csv --cem.scenarios.filename=/input_data/kub/scenarios_local/scenarios.json --cem.instance.time.start=0 --cem.instance.time.stop=86400 --cem.instance.time.step=3600 --cem.instance.postprocess.export.visualization.enabled=true --cem.instance.postprocess.export.report.enabled=true --cem.instance.postprocess.export.outputs.csv.enabled=false --cem.instance.postprocess.export.outputs.enabled=true --cem.instance.solar_shading.enabled=true --cem.instance.idealflows.enabled=true --cem.database.directory /exa5/data/d2024d05-047-users/euvincentc/apptainer_home/kub/e1c6da50/Paris_partitioned --directory /exa5/data/d2024d05-047-users/euvincentc/apptainer_home/kub/e1c6da50/Paris_partitioned --cem.instance.solar_shading.ray-tracing.quad-order 1

  During initialization at time: 0
  Tag: extended initialization.nonlinear[1]

  Common causes:
   * The system of equations has no solution - the residual will be above zero.
     - This may be caused by initial conditions not being fully specified, check the translation log.
     - In some cases the event-logic can cause this.
   * Starting values are too far from the solution, see homotopy in the manual.
     - In rare cases this could occur at events.
   * The equations are too discontinuous for the nonlinear solver - the residual will have knees.
     - Likely caused by over-using noEvent.
  Especially consider the first two items above when the nonlinear solver fails during initialization.

  To get more information consider the options:
